30/10/2020, 12:58â€¯am - Muhammad Ali Ijaz: So, the general announcement type stuff first.

Rector requested students to have number of security officer or office and report anything out of the ordinary immediately. There is a threat against universities especially NUST due to army link. Yesterday Islamic was also closed due to security threat. The added checks at gates are also due to this threat.

Rector said the purpose of Nust Student Forum is to bridge the gap between students and admin and this will be a regular thing with students reporting issues to their NSF representative and him/her forwarding it up through the concerned people towards the rector.

Rector also focused that mingling of day scholars and hostelites will not be tolerated and is a red line. 7 students have been expelled (not sure from uni or hostel) who were hostelites. Rector said from now on the day scholars will also be expelled. 

Coming to your issues first

*Internet*
Purpose of blocking of net services from 9-5 is not too force student to go to classes but to ease load on internet otherwise the online classes suffer. Still the speed has been increased from 2Mb to 5Mb from 9-5. Youtube has also been blocked due to online classes but it was also blocked on Saturday and rector told the concerned admin to unblock it for Saturdays. Signal of routers issue was raised and rector directed the concerned adm to fix it.

*Library*
Library will now be open on weekends for hostelites but not on day scholar days.

*Emergency Exit from Hostel*
Exit from hostels is only allowed in important cases. All requests will be approved by pro rector so please take care. Reasons that are valid to leave include shaadi of bhai/behen (not khaala cousin), death in same circle as the former, exams such as GAT, doctor appointments etc. There is a SOP for obtaining leave from hostel so please follow it. If you have an upcoming matter for which you need to leave inform timely. In case of emergency you can break SOP and directly call DD hostel waghera. Managers told students that they can leave but if they do not have quarantine rooms they canâ€™t come back. Rector strictly told DD Hostel to convey that rooms are available. Maam Maria (I think thatâ€™s her name) is a new manager type for female hostels so students can also contact her in case of issues.

*Sports*
Sports will now be allowed in hostels and in NUST (The latter only on hostelite days) but students are requested to keep distances and not make crowds.

*Khadija Hostel Water Issue*
Rector almost scolded the PMO adm for not fixing the Khadija hostel water issue. Apparently smell and different taste and students having health issues. Rector ordered it to be fixed at the earliest.

*Barber*
Rector has ordered concerned authorities to increase no of barbers and maybe tailors as well and also ensure the quality of barbers.

*Transport*
Action ordered on fees (students paying for 22 days while using only for 11), changing of drivers and general service of Baig Tpt.

*Audio and Video*
Uni has ordered better cameras and 360 voice sensitive mics at great expense, but they are being imported. Also, all classes wonâ€™t have them immediately. Priority will be given to those with studies that need more communication and explanation so hum thora ladder par neecha he hein.

Baaki aaga ka masla bhi batata rehna and ill keep forwarding them.
Thanks

24/02/2021, 1:03â€¯pm - Ahmad Noob: Dear Sir, 
With due respect, it is stated that the curfew timings currently in place are simply not fair. Keeping hostellites inside all day and letting them out for an hour and a half leaves us feelings less like students and more like inmates at a state penitentiary. To ignore the implications such policies would have on the mental health of students seems unfair. 

The last time such a complaint was made, the response we recieved was that DL mode is provided for those who cannot comply with the policies in place. Yet DL mode is only provided to those who have emergencies i.e health, family matters etc. Students that have no such excuse have to either deal with it, or give up their hostel rooms and become day scholars. Again, quite unfair. 

Mess workers, Hostel Managers, Teachers, Administration members, invigilators for the exams, all come to the university premises from outside. The only group of people that don't go outside of the university are the hostellites. Students interact with mess staff, managers, teachers that come in contact with day scholars and who themselves come from outside the university. A recurring theme emerges, mainly the hostellites being the only ones that are sacrificing, while the rest of the university is operating more or less as it once did. 

We realize that there is the threat of Covid-19, and that it is not something to be sniffed at. But the fact remains that these policies affect hostellites more than anyone else. We request that you revise the policies to be a bit more hostelite friendly. We have no quarrel with you. We simply want to live without the feeling of being prisoners. 

Regards, 
Hostellites

12/01/2023, 4:19â€¯pm - Shery: 1. FEA Exam will be same for all three sections. Course syllabus will be till Uniform distributed loading of beams
2. Focus only on details given in PPT slides, derivations which are not provided on slides will not be included

4. The theory 70% is sub-divided by 45% of final exam,30% of Mid, 15% of quizzes and 10% of assignments.
5. Most probably there will be 4 to 5 questions, including a case study in which all steps i.e. selection of elements, B.C  etc. needs to be explained and slected.

16/01/2023, 11:30â€¯pm - Shery: ESE marks have been uploaded on Qalam. Common mistakes are as follows; Q1 where shape functions for a 3-node bar element were to be derived; many students just couldn't write the correct polynomial function, some made two separate elements and then derived something, a few just did what was on slides. All of those got a zero. Q2 where a distributed load was given on beam elements and a spring element was attached. Most of the students failed to recognize that phi 2 dof was zero as there was no external value given nor there was a boundary condition (no reaction). Thus, failed to solve the problem after putting boundary conditions. Q3 part g was mostly wrong where it was asked that which type of stress should be used to analyse the tension, compression or shear. As discussed in class, either directional stresses with transformation or principal stresses were to be analysed.
